  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_96025aff-f117-46f1-a8d1-5a1a70360e48'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText4433953075793102873" style="display:none"><b>Heaven must be missing an angel....</b><br /><br />The angel Bethany and her mortal love, Xavier, have already pushed the boundaries of Heaven with their relationship. In this conclusion to the Halo trilogy, the two take their love to the next, forbidden, step: They marry.<br /><br />At a time when they believe nothing will come between them again, they are faced with their most daunting challenge yet: the Sevens, a military order of angels designed to maintain balance in the universe. These soldiers won't stop until their job is done - capture the wayward angel and send her home.<br /><br />Secrets, exile, and unexpected allies flavor the rest of this intense love story and adventure.<br /><br />Beth discovers there is only one way back to earth, but the cost is higher than she - and readers - ever imagined. If she can survive, she can prove to Heaven and Earth that there is nothing stronger than the power of love.</span>

<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/51763746-ashley-lynn"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1463001875i/51763746._UY100_CR25,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/51763746-ashley-lynn">Ashley Lynn</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">To go to heaven, you must live a life for God. I'm not saying that means you must live "sin free" but you just have to put your faith into Christ and <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">To go to heaven, you must live a life for God. I'm not saying that means you must live "sin free" but you just have to put your faith into Christ and accept him as your leader and Savior. There are many sins that one can commit and still get into Heaven. I know for a fact that i don't live a sin-free life, but i know that my 'spot in heaven' is still reserved because i accept Christ in my life. <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer205638199" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14600840336792271945">I just want to tell you all: this is the first book I really considered quitting not once, not twice, but <i> three times. </i> I am so happy that this series is over and that I will never pick up any of these books from this series again for as long as I live. I am the definition of done. <b> Also, spoilers will be abound and aplenty throughout this whole review, and this is going to a a mostly Supernatural gif-filled extravaganza, because A). That is how angels/demons/etc. should be done and B). I can. </b></span>
  <span id="freeText14600840336792271945" style="display:none">I just want to tell you all: this is the first book I really considered quitting not once, not twice, but <i> three times. </i> I am so happy that this series is over and that I will never pick up any of these books from this series again for as long as I live. I am the definition of done. <b> Also, spoilers will be abound and aplenty throughout this whole review, and this is going to a a mostly Supernatural gif-filled extravaganza, because A). That is how angels/demons/etc. should be done and B). I can. So if you do not like spoilers or Supernatural, leave now, because shit's about to get ugly up in here </b><br><br>I do not even really know where to start in the shit-fest that was Heaven, but I suppose where I started with all of my other reviews of this series, and the root of most of these book's problems: <i> Bethany. </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709555.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And even with <i> her </i> I don't really know where to start! First off, this is what Adornetto tries and <i> make </i> us believe that Bethany is going to be like in Heaven:<br><br><i>I let the timid girl I’d once been shrink into the shadows like a wallflower at a dance and allowed the new Beth to take over. I didn’t know her too well, but somehow I felt like she’d been there all along, waiting in the wings, an understudy ready for her moment to shine. </i><br><br>No. Just no. She is vapid, she is stupid, she is judgmental and critical of other females, she complains about every single thing that happens to her, and even when it's <i> not </i> about her and <i> she's </i> not even directly effected by it, she still somehow turns it around and makes it all about her. She is only "strong" when it is convenient for her to be, which is normally at the worst times literarily possible. Like this tidbit, for instance, right after she gets married to Xavier in a church with a priest, and first off, what the fuck is the priest even doing <i> marrying </i> them? It is told to us that he clearly knows what Bethany is and what they are doing and the repercussions of such actions, but he <i> does it anyways? </i> And what are the two of them even <i> doing </i> getting married in such an extremely religious way, anyways? They are already basically giving God a one-finger salute, and if they thought getting <i> married in this way </i> was going to somehow sooth the man upstairs, they were incredibly wrong. If anything, that's adding not only the one finger salute, but adding fireworks, a ten-piece band, and a huge, fluorescent sign with the words, "FUCK YOU" emblazoned onto them. So, the priest basically gets murdered by this reaper <s> which I think he totally deserved </s> and this is how Bethany reacts immediately afterwards about the man who basically <i> gave up his life for them. </i> And, let me remind you, we are supposed to think of her as strong now:<br><br><i> “Beth, what have we done?” he whispered. “We killed someone.” <b> “No, we didn’t.” </b> I knelt down beside him and took his hands in mine. “Listen to me, Xavier, <b> this isn’t our fault.”</b><br><br>“Get in,” she commanded. “Now.” <b> “No,” I objected, pulling feebly away from them. “I’m sick of everybody telling us what to do!” </b> “You have betrayed the laws of Heaven and caused the untimely death of a man of the cloth,” my sister said through clenched teeth. “Have you no regrets?” <b> “We didn’t know that would happen!” </b><br><br>We just wanted to be married. Why is that so wrong?” “In the eyes of Heaven it is,” Ivy said, her rainstorm eyes meeting mine calmly for the first time. <b>“That’s not fair,” </b> I protested, and at the same time felt tears threatening to spill. </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/393916.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Are you <i> kidding me?!?! </i> Are you fucking kidding me, Bethany?! How is it <i> not </i> your fault?! Because you two <s> idiots </s> decided to get married, the guy died. And you seriously didn't think that something like that just <i> might </i> happen? I'm not even an angel and I know that and angel/human shacking up, and then getting married is a pretty big deal, so you honestly didn't think that there would be some serious repercussions for your actions? And, Adornetto, how is this supposed to make me think of Bethany as anything other than a weak, spineless, little idiot, exactly? It's not like I'm inferring these things, you pretty much put them smack down on the page by calling her "feeble" and making her cry and complain about how much <i> her</i> life sucks when a guy just <i> died. </i> And then you have Gabriel say stuff like this!<br><br><i>“You do not experience emotion, Bethany— you wallow in it, you are controlled by it, and everything you have done is based entirely on self-interest.” <br><br>“Just because you don’t understand love doesn’t make it wrong!” “This isn’t about love anymore. It’s about obedience and responsibility. Two concepts you appear not to understand.”<br></i><br><br>First off, as a little aside, that made me want to like you Gabriel but then Adornetto had to go and mess it all up. As usual, which I will be talking about later. And everything Bethany <i> says </i> just makes me want to puke:<br><br><i>“We’ve never talked about it, you know,” he continued in a tentative voice. I knew he didn’t want to push me. “The time you spent in…” Xavier petered out. But I wasn’t afraid to say it. “Hell?” I prompted. “There’s not much to tell. It was everything they say it is.” <br><br>I saw a poster on a door that read WE LOVE OUR REBELS. I stopped for a moment and thought about it. Maybe I would fit in here because that was who I’d become now. A runaway. A rebel. But not without a cause. <br></i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Really, Bethany? Because <i> everyone </i> knows that Hell is full of nightclubs with massive sex orgies and 5-star hotels with suites where the demons and super speshul (AKA hot people from the orgy club) evil people can hang out with one another, and don't forget the random deserts here and there. We only saw the way Hell is normally portrayed once! <i> Once! </i> And that was for what? Ten pages? <i> Maybe? </i> First off, adding the "not without a cause" made everything before that sound so tacky that I couldn't even take any of it seriously. And what does Bethany think? That they are <i> actually </i> a bunch of rebels? Ole Miss is a very preppy southern college; just because that's their mascot/saying does <i> not mean </i> that the class populace are a bunch of nonconformists! And if anyone is actually questioning whether or not Bethany is <i> actually </i> as stupid as I say, here's a real gem for you:<br><br><i>“What’s wrong?” I was seized by a wave of self-consciousness. Had I done something wrong? I wracked my brain, trying to remember every move I’d made so far, but I’d been too lost in the moment to remember. “We don’t have protection. I didn’t think we’d need it.” “Forget it.” </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709557.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, Adornetto, just tell your young, female, audience that it is okay to have sex without protection, <i> because love and your hubby's ability to pull out quick enough will see you through! </i> <s> Just fucking kill me now </s> <br><br>And nothing bad still really ever happens to her through the whole damn book! Right after they are uprooted from Venus Cove, first they stay in a five-star resort cabin, and then guess where she gets to go, in case you guys couldn't tell, she gets to go to <i> Ole Miss. </i> And, what makes it all worse, is that they change identities and guess what they are listed as? <i> Brother and sister. </i> So guess what happens? Tons of judgmental attitude and slut-shaming from Bethany as Xavier gets hit on by every girl on campus, who it isn't even their fault that they didn't know that they were married, but Bethany hates them all, anyways:<br><br><i>“I’m glad you did,” Mary said in a high-pitched, fluty voice. I rolled my eyes behind her back. It was starting already. The female attention that Xavier received was going to get on my nerves fast. </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709558.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Stop it, Bethany. But does it? Nope. Because not only does the slut-shaming continue, but Bethany literally goes <i> crazy: </i><br><br><i> I slept fitfully from then on. I dreamed of Peyton and Xavier’s wedding, full of rapturous guests and bouquets of flowers just as it should be instead of substitute rings and a dead priest like ours had featured. Xavier’s entire family was there and Peyton’s father gave her away at the altar. Mary Ellen was there too, tugging on my sleeve incessantly and crying <b> this bitch is fucking crazy </b> when Xavier failed to acknowledge her presence. Then the scene shifted and I watched as Wade proposed to Molly. I saw her accept without hesitation and he carried her across the dance floor. She seemed to be dancing while standing on his feet so he was propping her up like a ragdoll. None of the moves she made were her own and her head lolled eerily to one side like she was a puppet full of stuffing. When her vacant eyes met mine, they were looking right through me <b> because this was all a dream, and did I mention I'm crazy?. </b> <br><br>"[I] snapped. I was not going to let this happen. Xavier and I had been through enough and there was no chance I was going to let some frivolous freshman screw up the one place that was still safe for us. I pointed a finger at Mary Ellen’s mouth and a second later a thick layer of skin began to creep across her lips <br><br>“Was that really necessary?” he hissed into my ear as he helped Mary Ellen to her feet. Ordinarily, I would have felt regret or guilt over what I’d done, but today I looked into Mary Ellen’s alarmed face and frightened eyes and felt nothing. Yes, it was necessary. <br></i><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/387618.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes I added parts for creative allowance, but can you really blame me? This girl is off her rocker. A few pears short of a fruit basket. You guys get what I mean. And, yes,<br><br>And, of course, Bethany is absolutely useless without Xavier. She literally cannot do anything without him, and threatens that she will <i> kill herself </i> if anything happens to him so many times that I wanted to puke my guts out (which I will also talk about later). But you know what <i> really </i> got to me? The way people treated her!<br><br><i>I held the elevator door for a woman carrying a cardboard box piled with pillows and picture frames. “Oh, I can wait,” she said emphatically. “You’re so nice and pretty, I don’t wanna mess you up.” <br> </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709559.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No real person who was actually struggling with their stuff would wait a whole extra elevator just to "not mess Bethany up!" And how would she even mess her up, anyways? It's walking into a goddamn elevator; just go stand in the corner so you don't run into anyone! Jesus! Adornetto does not need to make Bethany so special!<br><br>I need to move on, so now I will go to <b> Gabriel and Molly. </b><br><br>Yup, that's right, I said <i> Gabriel and Molly. </i> I wanted to like Gabriel so badly, since him and Ivy were basically the only ones that told Bethany how it actually was, but then Molly has to walk in with absolutely <i> no </i> redeeming qualities:<br><br><i>“Oh, just little things, Like how I should dress and how I shouldn’t speak to men who aren’t my husband.” She waved her hands at Xavier. “Don’t worry, you have a wife so you don’t count.” “Molly…You don’t have to believe everything they say.” “Well, actually, Wade is my fiancé. And I have to be obedient to him.” </i> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709560.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She is <i> so </i> incredibly stupid, and is in an incredibly abusive relationship with this jerk-off named Wade most of the book. Now, I am not against Angel-people romance, hell, I fell for it hook, line, and sinker with Angelfall, and in Supernatural I enjoy Cas' curiosity about sex <s>cough cough Pizza Man porn boner cough cough, </s> but if you're going to do it, you have to make it not only believable for Gabriel, an archangel no less, but for me to boot. And let me tell you, Gabriel would not fall for anyone like <i> Molly. </i> And what makes it worse is that the scene where he kisses her is so random:<br><br><i>“My life is governed by rules,” Gabriel said, almost to himself. Before any of us knew what was happening, Gabriel took Molly’s face in his hands, leaned down, and kissed her. </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709561.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At this point I was so done with this book if it hadn't been on my computer I would have chucked it across the room, but I'll just leave my final thoughts about this to the <i> real </i> Gabriel:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709562.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><s> Thank you Gabriel bby let me have your babies </s><br><br>Now, we get onto the writing. Everything that was supposed to be funny was not and everything that was supposed to be hilarious I found annoying. And let me tell you something; Adornetto is one of the worst sex writers I've ever seen:<br><br><i> Our first night as husband and wife felt like exploring a magical underwater world where nothing existed save the two of us. <br><br>..I still felt like I was diving from a great height. The same feelings from last night washed over me as I descended back into the coral sea of vivid colors and warm sensations, a place where only the two of us existed in a fantastical dimension. <br></i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709563.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>BAHAHAHAH ARE YOU FUCKING SERIOUS LIKE WHERE THE FUCK ARE WE THE LITTLE MERMAID OOH HO HO HO IT'S SO FUCKING WET LET ME JUST DIVE INTO YOUR DICK HERE XAVIER.<br><br>And when Mary saw the two of them making out in the locker rooms (they were supposed to be brother and sister), and The Seven, who I realized were basically just Slendermen just made me burst out laughing and go:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709564.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And I was never able to take anything seriously in this book ever again.<br><br>And the stuff that was supposed to be funny? Like when this scene happened?<br><br><i>“Reckon they’re vampires?” I heard one whisper. “Girl, you have got to stop watching True Blood,” her friend said, shaking her head in mock concern. Molly and Xavier shared a chuckle while Gabriel and I looked on blankly. Xavier patted my knee. “I’ll explain later.” </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709565.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I did not find funny at all.<br><br>And just the whole damn plot was ridiculous. Like I said earlier, nothing bad ever really happened to Bethany. Ever. The only thing that happened that I felt was actually horrible, Bethany losing her wings, was completely down-sized by Adornetto because Bethany <i> wanted </i> her wings off and, as she liked to whine about for the last ten percent of the book, <i> hated </i> Heaven and didn't even want to be there. So what the fuck bad actually happened to her. Really? Nothing, that's what. And the amount of loopholes when it came to Xavier; like the time that he died and <i> this </i> happened:<br><br><i> “I don’t know what I can do. He’s already gone.” “What!” I almost screamed at her. “You’ve done this before, you’ve brought people back! I've seen<br>you do it!” “People who were close to death,” my sister said. “On the brink. But he’s … past that point now.” “No…” I cut her off. “If he dies, I die.” " Okay." </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709566.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You can't just make loopholes like that! Just because Bethany threatens Ivy with suicide when Ivy said it was <i> impossible </i> does not make it automatically able to happen! And just everything with Xavier period. First he's dead, then he's fine, then he's possessed, and then he turns out to be some half-angel?! This just makes me so upset. Why can't just one person be a normal, intelligent, human being? Why is anyone that is special/smart not human? I don't like that some authors make people think they need to be angels/vampires/other creatures to be important or worth anything. Not that I don't want them, but just they way Adornetto objectifies humans and angels really bothered me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709567.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I hated Heaven, and am going to end my review with this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380358361i/709568.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380358361i/709569.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380358361i/709570.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Because happiness.<br><b> Pre-review </b><br><br>Something I just saw in this books synopsis is incredibly pissing me off; two parts of it, actually. First off, this quote:<br><br>" Only sixteen when she started the series, Ally Adornetto <b> knows how teen hearts beat.." </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No. And if you don't get it yet, fucking no. She does <i> not </i> know how teen hearts beat, if anything, she knows how to make teen hearts <i> stop </i> beating because their books literally kill you with their idiocy. I'll just direct you <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/160396380" rel="nofollow noopener"> my review of Hades </a> and <a> my review of Halo </a> to show you my rage over those two books, and you'll just have to scroll for not even two seconds to see the absolute <i> hatred </i> of what Adornetto has done in these books and with this series. I don't know who wrote that synopsis for this book, but either they've never really read the books or is being paid a lot of money to write something that would clearly be incredibly painful for me or just about anyone else I know. <br><br>And then, just the rest of the damn synopsis! I mean, what the hell!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What in the <i> Hell </i> is this?! They're actually going through with getting fucking <i> married?! </i> Just kill me now, because I can already tell that this book is going to be one of my most hated this year, if not <i> the </i> most hated. The plot in this already leaves me with questions. What in the hell happened with Hell?!?! Last time I knew, <s> the Colonel from KFC</s> Satan was still pretty pissed at her and wanted her ass dead, but now he's apparently <i> leaving her alone now?! </i> He's <i> the devil; </i> he doesn't give a damn if they're getting <i> married! </i> That's not how things work, Adornetto! You're creating a plot-hole the size of China, here, and it's pissing me off. And what the hell is God doing about all this?! The synopsis says "rouge angels" so I'm assuming they're aren't allied with God or even going against his wishes, so he's just totally cool with her <i> marrying a human and possibility producing Nephilim children?! </i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fucking. No. I understand the need for creative license and all that, but she's taking it too far. Honestly, I'm rooting for those "rouge" angels! They're the only ones actually doing the job they're meant to do! Seriously, though, they should be called the "correct" angels, and everyone else who's just rooting or even passively ignoring this stupid relationship like God apparently is should be the rouge ones. All of them, besides those seven angels, are failing at the job of <i> being </i> angels. I hope they drag Bethany's ass to Heaven and hopefully God suddenly remembers the fucking Bible and punishes that idiot. This fills me with so much rage I think I'll just let Sokka explain my feelings for this. Sokka?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380358361ra/709574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Thank you, Sokka. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14600840336792271945" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer224660330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13458349234208683233">As of 7/9/2012<br/><br/>So I finally got around to reading (and trying to make sense of) the synopsis.<br/><br/><i>Only sixteen when she started the series, Ally Adornetto knows how teen hearts beat,</i><br/><br/>You see, this is the obvious bait. I'm not going to take it. I'm going to walk away and move on to the next sentence, because if I were to even get started on how much of an insult this is to teenagers (and really every human being on the planet) I wouldn't be able to stop. And none of us want that.<br/><br/>So instead I'm going to </span>
  <span id="freeText13458349234208683233" style="display:none">As of 7/9/2012<br><br>So I finally got around to reading (and trying to make sense of) the synopsis.<br><br><i>Only sixteen when she started the series, Ally Adornetto knows how teen hearts beat,</i><br><br>You see, this is the obvious bait. I'm not going to take it. I'm going to walk away and move on to the next sentence, because if I were to even get started on how much of an insult this is to teenagers (and really every human being on the planet) I wouldn't be able to stop. And none of us want that.<br><br>So instead I'm going to take this the literal way and say that I hope Adornetto knows about the blood pumping processes of the heart, teenage or otherwise. Because that would at least ensure that she has the basic biological knowledge of a third grader.<br><br><i>Bethany, an angel sent to Earth, and her mortal boyfriend, Xavier, have been to Hell and back. But now their love will be put to its highest test yet, as they defy Heavenly law and marry.</i><br><br>I mean, really, this is literally the stupidest thing I've read all week. It just, I can't, I can't do it. It hurts when I think about this for too long.<br><br>I really can't understand why<br><br>I just don't<br><br>help<br><br>Okay, I'm going to try to make logic out of this.<br><br>So I guess Adornetto is trying to go for the Nephilim thing here?<br><br>But the problem is, and I'm not positive, the <i>reason why</i> God didn't want any angels marrying humans is because they always had kids and those kids were... Nephilim.<br><br>So, to me at least, it seems that as long as Bethie and Xavier agree to adopt nobody should really give a shit.<br><br>And it's not like, even in the bible, you saw God getting all flustered about the whole thing. I mean he kind of let them do it anyway, right, so it must not have been <i>that</i> big of a deal.<br><br><i>They don’t tell Beth’s archangel siblings, Gabriel and Ivy, but the angels know soon enough, and punishment comes in a terrifying form: the Sevens, who are rogue angels bent on keeping Beth and Xavier apart, destroying Gabriel and Ivy, and darkening angelic power in the heavens.</i><br><br>Wait, okay, what, this is the part where it really starts to not make sense.<br><br>If the Sevens are rogue.<br><br>And the rogue are, like, not with God. (I assume that's why they're labelled as rogue.)<br><br>And God is not with Xavier and Bethie getting married.<br><br>Shouldn't the Sevens not care?<br><br>And even if I've got it all wrong, and the Sevens are really with God, there is still no reason as to why it's such a big deal. <i>Who cares?</i> Oh god, no pun intended, I just can't understand why anyone gives a fuck. It's just so hard for me to care, why would they? Don't they have more important things to do with their time than dabble in the lives of two very annoying brats?<br><br>AND IF THE SEVEN ARE BENT ON 'DARKENING ANGELIC POWER' THEN, UH, DISOBEYING GOD WOULD BE A REALLY GOOD PLACE TO START WITH THAT.<br><br><i>The only way Bethany and Xavier can elude the Sevens is to hide in the open</i><br><br>What the fuck? HOW DOES THIS MAKE ANY SENSE??!!?!??!<br><br>The only way they can <i>evade</i> the Sevens is to HIDE IN BROAD DAYLIGHT????<br><br>AOGJ;LERABIVAP;,O;KJETHAJO,O I DON'T UNDERSTAND HELP<br><br><i>Gabriel and Ivy set them up at college, where they can’t reveal their relationship,</i><br><br>HUH? WHY?<br><br>Look if there are a group of dangerous angels on your tail then NOT MAKING KISSY FACES AT EACH OTHER EVERY FIVE SECONDS ISN'T GOING TO HELP THEM FROM FIGURING OUT WHO YOU ARE.<br><br>And they could very, very easily just have a relationship<br><br>IN<br><br>PRIVATE<br><br>LIKE OTHER PEOPLE WHO CAN'T BE TOGETHER IN PUBLIC DO<br><br>EVERY DAY<br><br>WHY AM I EVEN ARGUING LOGIC WITH THIS BOOK<br><br>AND WHY AM I TALKING IN CAPS AND NOT USING ANY PUNCTUATION<br><br>UGH<br><br>SORRY<br><br><i>Will Bethany be called back to Heaven – forever – and face leaving the love of her life?</i><br><br>OH MY GOD WHO GIVES A SHIT.<br><br>First of all we built the entire fucking synopsis up to this pathetic ending and sad excuse for a conflict (trust me, I know it's hard to write conflict, but this just sucks). Second of all <i>every single problem</i> Bethie and Xavier face could be simply enough solved or doesn't make any logical sense.<br><br>Third of all... THAT ISN'T ANY REAL CONFLICT.<br><br>I mean okay look<br><br>It's like either she's called back to Heaven... or she isn't.<br><br>Either God tells her to bring her feathery tail back up to the clouds... <i>or he doesn't.</i><br><br>THAT ISN'T CONFLICT.<br><br>THAT ISN'T EVEN A CHOICE THAT BETHANY HAS TO MAKE, HOW IS THAT CONFLICT.<br><br>WHY AM I STILL TRYING TO ARGUE LOGIC INTO THIS BOOK.<br><br>WHY AM I ANGRY THAT THIS WHOLE SERIES IS A HUGE GLOP OF BORING BULLSHIT WRITTEN BY AN UNINTELLIGENT UNEDUCATED PERSON WHO'S PRESENTED AS A SPOKESPERSON FOR ALL TEENAGERS<br><br>I MEAN I WENT THROUGH THIS WHOLE THING<br><br>WHEN I READ HADES<br><br>AND NOW I'M DOING IT AGAIN<br><br>LIKE A SICK CYCLE<br><br>UGH<br><br><br>As of 4/10/2012 <b>EXTRA EXTRA BIG WARNING DUE TO EXCESS OF TROLLS: THE FOLLOWING CONSISTS OF SWEARING, HATE DIRECTED TOWARDS THE HALO SERIES BY ALEXANDRA ADORNETTO, GENERAL DISTASTE FOR PEOPLE WHO RATED THE BOOK FIVE STARS BEFORE THE COVER HAD EVEN CAME OUT YET, GIFS, AND MOST IMPORTANTLY SWEARING AND ANGER.<br><br>IF YOU LIKE THE HALO SERIES IN ANY WAY YOU SHOULD PROBABLY NOT CONTINUE. IF YOU'RE LOOKING FOR A TASTEFUL, CLEAN PRE-REVIEW OF THIS BOOK THEN YOU SHOULD NOT PROCEED. IF YOU ARE UNDER 12 THEN YOU SHOULD PROBABLY NOT PROCEED. <br><br>(Not like I can stop you if you are under 12 and decide to proceed anyway, though.)<br><br>MOST IMPORTANTLY, IF YOU ARE A FAN OF THE HALO SERIES <u>DO. NOT. PROCEED.</u> AT ALL. AND IF YOU DO PROCEED ANYWAY, NO LECTURING ON HOW GREAT OF A WRITER ADDIE IS AND HOW I NEED TO STFU, M'KAY? M'KAY!</b><br><br><br><br><br>Warning: Will be flipping out. Halo...<i>does things to me...</i><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>HOLY FUCKING SHIT. WHAT THE FUCKEDY FUCK.<br><br>Why, why, JESUS FUCKING CHRIST WHY IS THIS <i>MONSTER</i> RATED SO HIGH?<br><br>THE SHIT HASN'T EVEN COME OUT YET!<br><br>To combat all of the morons rating this book five or so stars before the motherfucking cover is even released, I'll be rating this bastard one, one, A SINGULAR star even though I wish I could give it NOTHING.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380361457ra/712458.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>"You get NOTHING! You LOSE! <i>GOOD DAY, SIR</i>!"<br><br>STOP RATING BOOKS YOU HAVEN'T READ, PEOPLE. ESPECIALLY BOOKS IN CRAPPY, PREACHY, NASTY SERIES'S LIKE THIS.<br><br>*cries*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380250664ra/681983.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>In this bloody <i>creature</i> of a series, I wish the average rating was fucking ONE STAR so there would be TRUTH about this <i>THING</i> everywhere on the planet!<br><br>*more crying*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380250664ra/681984.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>*even more crying*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380361457ra/712459.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>...<br><br><br>...<br><br><br>...</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13519037071881999764">RAAAAAAHHHHHHHGGGRRRRAAAAAAAHHHHH!!<br/><br/>FUCKING PIECE OF ROTTING BULLSHIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIT!!!!!<br/><br/>AHAAAHAAAAHAAAAAHHAAAA!! HAHAAAHAAA!!<br/><br/>(You see what this series has done to me.<br/>It's driven me crazy... 0.0)<br/><br/><br/>WHHHHYYY!? WHY, WHY, WHY, WHY, WHHHHHYYYYEEEEE?<br/><br/><i><br/><br/>FUCK THE WORLD!!!! DX<br/><br/><br/>Update: 3/21/12<br/><br/>I just read the synopsis. Is this for real? Really?<br/><br/><b>REALLY!?</b><br/><br/>So, in order to remain safe from some oooh scary angels, Bethany and Xavier go to college!? Oh sure, just blow $100,000 and party and whatnot! I am working my ASS </i></span>
  <span id="freeText13519037071881999764" style="display:none">RAAAAAAHHHHHHHGGGRRRRAAAAAAAHHHHH!!<br /><br />FUCKING PIECE OF ROTTING BULLSHIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIT!!!!!<br /><br />AHAAAHAAAAHAAAAAHHAAAA!! HAHAAAHAAA!!<br /><br />(You see what this series has done to me.<br />It's driven me crazy... 0.0)<br /><br /><br />WHHHHYYY!? WHY, WHY, WHY, WHY, WHHHHHYYYYEEEEE?<br /><br /><i><br /><br />FUCK THE WORLD!!!! DX<br /><br /><br />Update: 3/21/12<br /><br />I just read the synopsis. Is this for real? Really?<br /><br /><b>REALLY!?</b><br /><br />So, in order to remain safe from some oooh scary angels, Bethany and Xavier go to college!? Oh sure, just blow $100,000 and party and whatnot! I am working my ASS off just to afford the first year! You know what, fuck you!! You are going to college to hide while I am trying to go to college to LEARN and to better my FUCKING LIFE! <br /><br />GODMOTHERFUCKINGDAMMIT!!!<br /><br />(sorry, it's that time of the year when I am impatiently waiting to hear from the rest of the colleges I applied to and researching thousands of scholarships. It's a stressful time. -_-)<br /><br />I am so glad I am not reading this shit. I hope Bethany gets what she's always wanted and gets her wings ripped off so that she can stay with Xavier as a mortal and DIE!! BAHAHAHAHAHA!! XD<br /><br />Edit: 4/1/12<br />*stares at cover*<br /><br />Is... Is this for real? Is this the actual cover?<br /><br />........<br /><br />BAHAHAHAHA!! AHAHAHAHAHA!! *snorts* AHAHAHA!!<br /><br />*falls on the ground and kicks feet in the air* Teeheehee! Oh my god... Ha, ha, heh... That seals it, there is no god damn way I am getting this. I was worried that if the cover was too beautiful that I would have to get it. But this cover...!<br /><br />*points at cover and laughs more*<br /><br />Just go away! You are killing me! <br /><br />Edit: 8/1/12<br />So I read the first chapter because a friend of mine gave me a link to it. At first, I didn't even want to read it. I had sworn that I would not even glance in this hideous book's direction, that I would plug my ears and sing, "La la la la!" if anyone mentioned it's name.<br /><br /><br /><br />However, curiosity got the better of me.<br /><br /><br />UGH.<br /><br /><br />Yet, in a way, I am glad I read the first chapter. It helped me see what direction the book will go, and I do NOT want to go down the same path with this shit.<br /><br />So its starts out where Hades left off. There is an earthquake, the ring falls to the floor, and Bethany is preparing to be sent back to Heaven or whatever.<br /><br />But then the earthquake stops, and everything is honey-dorey.<br /><br />Are you kidding me!? Hades left us hanging on an "oh-so-intense-moment" where we think something bad is going to happen, then its just ends!? But I suppose I expected this. Ally has a thing for over-dramatizing every little thing when, in reality, nobody gives a flying fuck.<br /><br />After the little, "Oh it was just a warning tremor from God or whatever, no biggie!" Xavier and Bethany go to the church to get married. I noticed that the writing improved, but I still found myself skipping paragraphs and details here and there. Does the author have to explain every action of the characters and detail of the surroundings? I think I get the picture, Ally. I have imagination, you know!<br /><br />So Father Mel holds the ceremony, and woohoo, Bethany and Xavier are married. I got up from the computer at that point and asked myself, "Do I dare continue with this atrocity?" I noticed I didn't have much longer to go, so I took a deep breath and continued on reading. <br /><br />Then it (finally) started to get interesting. A Grim Reaper holding a scythe comes marching into the church. At first, I am all like, "Cool!" since I am a huge fan of Death and the Grim Reaper. I am hopping up and down in my chair, hoping that the Reaper has come to take Bethany or Xavier's soul (or maybe both, since I equally hate them) and exact punishment on them. But then the Grim Reaper turns on Father Mel, basically blaming him that Bethany got married to a mortal. He takes Father Mel's soul, and leaves the real culprits behind.<br /><br />WHAT THE FUCK!!?<br /><br />I hate this Grim Reaper! Why did he have to take it out on poor Father Mel!? Bethany is to blame! She started this whole mess!! I JUST DON'T GET IT AAAAAAGRRAAAJNGONDOGNINAISFN!! I WANT HER TO DIIIIIEEEEEE!!<br /><br /><br />So I am done. I can't... I just can't. Reading that first chapter completely sealed it. Done. Finito! I hate Bethany so much it makes me want to tear my hair out. I despise Xavier with a passion that I did not know I could ever feel. And I can no longer tolerate this stupid, pointless, aggravating, insulting, blasphemous, horrible, atrocious series any longer. This is the reason I no longer carry hope for the YA genre, when books like these get published and idolized, when people with actual talent get dismissed or ignored. <br /><br />I will not read this... thing... I never will. I already have an ending tot his series, and I am sticking to it.<br /><br />MY version of the conclusion to this series:<br /><br />God- You are no longer fit to be my messenger! I strip you of your powers, your wings, and your place in Heaven!<br />Bethany- Nooooooooooooo!<br />(She gets banished, her get ripped off, and she is sent back to Earth as a mortal)<br />Xavier-Beth! What happened!?<br />Bethany-I am no longer an angel...(sobs briefly)... I am like you now. We can be together, and grow old.<br />Xavier-We can... Oh, Beth. We will be together till then end.<br />Bethany-Yes, and we--<br />(A bus runs over her. After that, she gets trampled by stampeding cows. Then, a group of bicyclists speed over her crumpled body. She dies)<br />Xavier-Nooooooooo! Why, God, why--!?<br />(Xavier gets struck by lightning. He dies)<br />God-That will shut him up. :&gt;<br /><br />The End<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></i></span>

<div id="review_213264979" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/213264979" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6365324-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1377624284p2/6365324.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/6365324-angela">Angela</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer213264979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17050328800893087514">For some reason, there is a lot of bad review. I like the book because I love all book. The author work hard for it. And i'm mad that people are being ass. You can dislike the book but you don't have to be bitchy about it. How would you like it if you write your own book, and you get a hell of hate message? But again, i'm no one side. Although in my other side, i guess that this "hate" message to Alexandra Adornetto can enlight her to do better in future writing. Sign.... people these day... i d</span>
  <span id="freeText17050328800893087514" style="display:none">For some reason, there is a lot of bad review. I like the book because I love all book. The author work hard for it. And i'm mad that people are being ass. You can dislike the book but you don't have to be bitchy about it. How would you like it if you write your own book, and you get a hell of hate message? But again, i'm no one side. Although in my other side, i guess that this "hate" message to Alexandra Adornetto can enlight her to do better in future writing. Sign.... people these day... i don't know what to say anymore. <br /><br /> In the beginning, I was just annoyed with the main character Beth, because she still act childish and very stubborn. But doing all of this and why she have to do for her beloved make me like her even more. She sweet and strong. Her love for Xavier and going against Heaven for what she truly fights for is the reason why I really respect her. <br />	Even if the story end beautifully and very teary, I still felt that there some thing that still need to be explain. The relationship with Archangel Gabriel and Molly? What the hell happened to them? Ah, It impossible to write how the Archangel such as him would fall in love. I don’t think she (the author) can take the risk of explain how that could happen. But it could that she make the reader VERY curious for sure. <br />	Overall, I like the second better with Jake. It was very intense. But I would prefer this book over the first one. The ending and the whole setting was just beautifully well written. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText8394876943896290134" style="display:none">Now, I'm not one to draw anatomy correctly 24/7...but at least I know how to critique myself and find my faults. <b>A COVER LIKE THIS HURTS ME</b>.<br /><br />That is THE tiniest ribcage I have ever seen, and her neck looks way awkward arched like that. Also, I haven't seen someone so tiny about the waist since Ariel the mermaid. For serious.<br />And I didn't know hair could be wings. That must be a new development in angel anatomy. The silhouette should also still imply foreshortening with arm muscles and size and whatnot, but here, Bethany's arms look like they belong to a five year-old.<br /><br />I wanna learn how to bend like that without strain.<br />That's my new goal.<br /><br />Also, Xavier's got <i>quite</i> the pointy moobs.<br /><br />...okay I'm done.</span>

<div id="review_396982862" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/396982862" />
    <a title="Mitch" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8170554-mitch"><img alt="Mitch" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396208595p2/8170554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/396982862?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mitch" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mitch" href="/user/show/8170554-mitch">Mitch</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8170554-mitch?shelf=no-just-no">no-just-no</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer396982862" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4012787279506500819">Ugh. Here I was thinking, hey, <i>Heaven</i> can't be so bad if I read it as a parody, right? Right? *Crickets* Who am I kidding, it's still terrible. The only thing that's remotely amazing is how I've now managed to finish this series even though I couldn't get past chapter four of the eye gouging turd that was <i>Fallen</i>, but that's neither here nor there. Only means this book isn't the biggest pile of crap, but it's still a pile of crap.<br/><br/>Where to start? Not a revelation at all, after <i>Halo</i> and <i>Hades</i> it's </span>
  <span id="freeText4012787279506500819" style="display:none">Ugh. Here I was thinking, hey, <i>Heaven</i> can't be so bad if I read it as a parody, right? Right? *Crickets* Who am I kidding, it's still terrible. The only thing that's remotely amazing is how I've now managed to finish this series even though I couldn't get past chapter four of the eye gouging turd that was <i>Fallen</i>, but that's neither here nor there. Only means this book isn't the biggest pile of crap, but it's still a pile of crap.<br /><br />Where to start? Not a revelation at all, after <i>Halo</i> and <i>Hades</i> it's really to be expected, but I'll go ahead and confirm this last installment is as filled with the same melodramatic writing, laughably bad dialogue, and ridiculously overwritten prose as its predecessors. Except this time, renegade angel Bethany finally marries longtime flame Xavier, so Adornetto gets to replace her standard cheesy lines with bizarre over the top exchanges that even I had to reread several times because, sorry, I don't get it. Then I just decided I didn't need to be enlightened about the intricacies of teen marriage and gave up. <br /><br />Consider the following:<br /><blockquote>“I want to kiss you,” I said suddenly. “I want to kiss my husband.”<br />“I think you need a distraction.” Xavier sighed.<br />“I completely agree....”<br />“Not that kind of distraction.”</blockquote><br />Ummm WTF. As if Beth's preachy attitude and teen marriage as a gesture of eternal love obsession aren't enough *shudders*, I get lines like - I don't even know what that is. Take it from here, Gabriel (yes he actually says this to Beth):<br /><blockquote>“You’re delusional.”</blockquote><br />Yup. I mean, Adornetto just keeps adding fuel to the fire, like, come on Beth, don't you know how a safe house works? Ummm, when Gabriel AND Ivy tell you to stay indoors, you DO NOT get Xavier to agree to let you wander around the yard and then turn it into a jaunt in the forest so the killer angels after you, who you know are nearby, can find and kill you. And judging Molly when she gets engaged because her relationship is totally different from yours, right? I ... just ... can't. <br /><br />But Bethany isn't even the worst thing about <i>Heaven</i>, I survived two books with her so far after all, what's more troubling is how the schizophrenic storytelling has gotten even worse - much worse. Beth and the gang go from hiding in the woods to hiding on a college campus to finally hiding in their hometown (umm WTF didn't they all agree at the beginning that staying in Venus Cove was a BAD idea?), and somewhere in the middle Lucifer pops up with Jake Thorn in tow, all connected by the most tenuous of logical connections and featuring pointless scenes like Beth and Xavier posing at siblings in college (because there will be a make out scene that somebody will interpret as incest, duh), Beth and Xavier making out in the woods (even though the angels on their tail can supposedly easily track them unless they're indoors or hiding among a whole bunch of people ... also, must resist dirty pun involving Xavier's last name), Beth dealing with her high energy err perky roommate, Mary Ellen, and Xavier falling for fellow college student Peyton, leading to this bizarre ... I don't even know how to describe this dream sequence:<br /><blockquote>I dreamed of Peyton and Xavier’s wedding, full of rapturous guests and bouquets of flowers just as it should be instead of substitute rings and a dead priest like ours had featured. Xavier’s entire family was there and Peyton’s father gave her away at the altar. Mary Ellen was there too, tugging on my sleeve incessantly and crying when Xavier failed to acknowledge her presence.</blockquote><br />Except Peyton's dropped right after whatever that was and never seen again while Adornetto goes back to dredging up every single college cliche, stereotype, and oversimplified misconception she can think of, sororities, Rush Week, the freshman fifteen ... come on, I've been in college longer than I've been out of college, let's get real. <br /><br />Then, there are the indescribably bizarre gems, oh wait, once again I have just the quote:<br /><blockquote>“Gracious!” Xavier exclaimed loudly. “So much for sticking together. What a bad wife.”</blockquote><br />That alone deserves an extra half star for this book (rounded down), I don't know how I could've have survived otherwise, because at this point the warning signs in my head are all saying in big bold letters, who's editing this? Is anyone editing this? Why would anyone willingly edit this? There are so many plot holes it's not even funny - besides the make out session in the woods that goes against common sense and every warning from Gabriel and Ivy, let's see, while Beth and Xavier are hiding in the cabin, Gabriel and Ivy go out but leave the keys to their jeep behind, a couple of days pass, then the two angels drive back in the jeep ... the same day they left! Or, Ivy and Gabriel leave Beth and Xavier alone in a room, and then, three paragraphs later, Beth starts talking to Gabe again! Wait, WTF?<br /><br />Even Beth admits it:<br /><blockquote>“Great. This is so messed up.”</blockquote><br />Yeah, pretty much. Lampshading. Let's just say this series ends with a huge deus ex machina cop out and I just wasted hours of my life I'll never get back. *Head desk*<br /><br />Oh, and I just looked at the cover. Am I the only one who notices her neck is abnormally long?</span>
  <a data-text-id="4012787279506500819" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14443553192736456336" style="display:none"><b>READ</b><br /><br />Raphael belongs to the SWAG club.<br /><br /><br />WHAT HAVE I DONE? SWEET SIGNLESS IN A MOTHERFUCKING DREAM BUBBLE, I AM GOING TO KILL MYSELF.<br /><br />Okay, what the fuck was this story about? What was the moral even supposed to be?<br /><br /><i> "Let's all get married at a young age, have sex, then give up everything for a man!"</i>- Alexandra Adornetto (But not really)<br /><br />This sums up my feelings:<br /><br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.google.com/imgres?num=10&amp;hl=en&amp;biw=1366&amp;bih=587&amp;tbm=isch&amp;tbnid=RqxyT1i73kGzGM:&amp;imgrefurl=http://jbriner.tumblr.com/post/8961361026/asksassydolorosa-i-love-all-the-sassy&amp;docid=KMHdECV2WqeLAM&amp;imgurl=http://media.tumblr.com/tumblr_lpye8uqjy41qcrd91.gif&amp;w=454&amp;h=539&amp;ei=y95fUIyvLK6PigKh-oHYCA&amp;zoom=1&amp;iact=hc&amp;vpx=84&amp;vpy=227&amp;dur=1104&amp;hovh=245&amp;hovw=206&amp;tx=129&amp;ty=153&amp;sig=104149084051155633162&amp;page=1&amp;tbnh=112&amp;tbnw=94&amp;start=0&amp;ndsp=26&amp;ved=1t:429,r:9,s:0,i:102">http://www.google.com/imgres?num=10&a...</a><br /><br />Also, this:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.google.com/imgres?num=10&amp;hl=en&amp;biw=1366&amp;bih=587&amp;tbm=isch&amp;tbnid=O-AaeVMVWLYrOM:&amp;imgrefurl=http://jbriner.tumblr.com/post/8961361026/asksassydolorosa-i-love-all-the-sassy&amp;docid=KMHdECV2WqeLAM&amp;imgurl=http://media.tumblr.com/tumblr_lpye91sfxG1qcrd91.gif&amp;w=500&amp;h=391&amp;ei=y95fUIyvLK6PigKh-oHYCA&amp;zoom=1&amp;iact=hc&amp;vpx=1038&amp;vpy=137&amp;dur=1048&amp;hovh=198&amp;hovw=254&amp;tx=154&amp;ty=111&amp;sig=104149084051155633162&amp;page=1&amp;tbnh=117&amp;tbnw=148&amp;start=0&amp;ndsp=26&amp;ved=1t:429,r:8,s:0,i:98">http://www.google.com/imgres?num=10&a...</a><br /><br />Yeah, Dolorosa does not approve of this message. And neither do I.<br /><br />Okay, let's continue.<br /><br />What the hell was up with rehab Heaven? All I could think of was Alcoholics Anonymous. What was the point of rehab Heaven? Why do people suddenly think it's okay to make Heaven into a weird ass place? You know, as a believer of God, I find this book offensive.<br /><br />This book mocks Christianity and shits in its face. And what Emily said about Bethany and Xavier is true. Those mofos are way too co-dependent.<br /><br />Thank God this series is over. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><b>**EDIT/CURRENTLY READING***</b><br /><br />The bitch put it in there. The fucking comment about marriage is a bond between a woman and a man who love each other. <br /><br />Let's begin the rant.<br /><br />Dear Adornetto, marriage is not <i>only</i> about love. People marry for money, when they are pressured, and what about those drunk marriages like Britney Spears'? Exactly, I think I've proved my point.<br />Also, if two homosexuals love each other, who are you to judge them and condescend them for wanting to marry each other? You talk about God, but obviously you're quick to judge. You're not God.<br /><br />Adornetto gives a bad name to Christians. She really does. She has spit on the face of angels. Since when did Raphael have swag? REALLY? Raphael is not some wanna be ghetto kid, okay?<br /><br />Thank you ver FUCKING much. And really, angel sex? Also, why the fuck doesn't Bethany feel and pain when she's having sex for the first time? Honestly, Adornetto, if you're a virgin and you're going to write a sex scene, do it right and research. DUH, logic.<br /><br />You write blasphemy, Adornetto.<br /><br />And the cover is still as ugly as fuck.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Ahh, hell naw, I'm too sober fo' this<br /><br />*Grabs a six pack of Sam Adams* That's better.<br /><br />So, what do I think of this book? <br /><br />The cover? Xavier has some nice titties...dayum, can I have them? *Takes a swig*<br /><br />Bethany?<br /><br />THE FUCK IS THAT? That looks NOTHING, and I mean, nothing like an angel. It's a....dinosaur? Nah, looks like wings over the sun, and look, they're making a heart over the evil sun.<br /><br />*Takes another swig*<br /><br />I'm an airship pirate, the only airship pirate....<br /><br />I KNOW this book is going to be bad.<br /><br /><br />UPDATE... I decided to have a go at commenting the sypnosis of this book...remember, I'm 'A Goth Reads My Immortal'...yes, I came up with that commentary that was lovely, but short lived... LET'S COMMENT!<br /><br /><br />"Only sixteen when she started the series<b>(I began writing my book when I was fourteen...I'm twenty and I still haven't finished writing my book)</b> Ally Adornetto knows how teen hearts beat<b>(Really? No, no she doesn't)</b>, and this long-awaited conclusion is certain to be her most popular book yet. <b>(Most popular to flame)</b><br /><br />Bethany, an angel sent to Earth, and her mortal boyfriend, Xavier, have been to Hell and back<b>(Hahahahahaha)</b>. But now their love will be put to its highest test yet<b>(When Bethany discovers she's pregnant)</b>, as they defy Heavenly law and marry<b>(Best angel EVER)</b>. They don’t tell Beth’s archangel siblings, Gabriel and Ivy, but the angels know soon enough, and punishment comes in a terrifying form: the Sevens<b>(Who are loosely based on the seven deadly sins)</b>, who are rogue angels<b>(RESEARCH, ADORNETTO)</b> bent on keeping Beth and Xavier apart, destroying Gabriel and Ivy, and darkening angelic power in the heavens.<b>(What was your first clue? Seven deadly sins?)</b><br /><br />The only way Bethany and Xavier can elude the Sevens is to hide in the open, and blend in with other mortals their own age<b>(Haven't they already been doing that?)</b>. Gabriel and Ivy set them up at college, where they can’t reveal their relationship, and where there is still danger around each corner. Will Bethany be called back to Heaven – forever – and face leaving the love of her life?<b>(Yes, please)</b>"</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer423408413" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6295487321945903738">I thought it couldn't get any worse. Boy, I was wrong.<br/><br/>Bethany Church, or the Paranormal Mary Sue, whichever you want to call her, hasn't changed. At all.<br/><br/>After Xavier proposed to Bethany at the end of <i>Hades</i>, God made it really clear that this marriage was an abomination. Did Xavier and Bethany listen? Of course not.<br/>So, they get married, cheese cheese blah blah, and OMG! A reaper appears to destroy it. What should they do? Bethany protects Xavier which made the reaper KILL Father Mel, Xavier's fam</span>
  <span id="freeText6295487321945903738" style="display:none">I thought it couldn't get any worse. Boy, I was wrong.<br><br>Bethany Church, or the Paranormal Mary Sue, whichever you want to call her, hasn't changed. At all.<br><br>After Xavier proposed to Bethany at the end of <i>Hades</i>, God made it really clear that this marriage was an abomination. Did Xavier and Bethany listen? Of course not.<br>So, they get married, cheese cheese blah blah, and OMG! A reaper appears to destroy it. What should they do? Bethany protects Xavier which made the reaper KILL Father Mel, Xavier's family friend!<br>DID I JUST READ THAT RIGHT? BETHANY, AN ANGEL, KILLED SOMEBODY! Okay, not directly, but she caused it.<br>Her response after Gabriel and Ivy arrived? <i>“We didn't know it would happen!”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380370787ra/723692.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*sighs* Bethany, you marry a human, which is prohibited by Heaven law, and you <i>didn't know it would happen?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387872ra/748180.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I doubt that Bethany will realize that, though.</i><br><br>So, Gabriel and Ivy tried to reason with her but she. Won't. Listen.<br><br><i>"But why? This is not fair! We only wanted to get married! Why can everyone see this from our perspective? What we have is TRUE LOVE!!"</i><br><br>Selfish, is Bethany's new name.<br><br>The new plan is to hide them because a group of Slenderman-like angels, the Sevens, are out to destroy them. Thanks a lot, Bethany, your stupid actions caused a lot of chaos.<br><br><i>"But I didn't mean it!"</i><br><br>Fuck you and shut up.<br><br>Gabriel and Ivy produced new identifications (which is impossible considering it was made in no time) so they could pass as brother and sister in Oxford. Okay, pause. That's impossible. You can't just go to college without filling out applications. It takes time, damn it! Something that Adornetto doesn't seem to understand!<br><br>So, they get into college and Bethany gets a roommate, Mary-Ellen, which is another excuse to mock teenage girls and their "sins" once again.<br>Blah blah blah, more drama with a popular girl wanting Xavier, blah blah blah, a bonfire and--<br>*record scratches*<br><br>Bethany and Xavier HAVE SEX.<br>Oh, no.<br><br>The worst part is, they decided not to use a condom because "Forget about it!" So much for the abomination of Nephilim.<br><br>Blah blah blah, AND MOLLY IS BACK ON THE PLOT! Really? <br>She moves to Oxford so she could get together with this creepy, controlling, guy named Wade.<br>She's SO over Gabriel, y'all.<br><br>Oh, talking about "y'all", Adornetto couldn't help but stereotype Southern people. Yes, really.<br><br>NOTHING CHANGED.<br><br>Then, Hell breaks loose over Xavier and Bethany's marriage (Wtf?) and like, always, Bethany is being selfish.<br><br><i>I felt my stomach sink to my shoes. Was this my fault? Were people now dying because of me, because I'd been stupid enough to make Lucifer angry?</i><br><br>Yes, Bethany. Thanks for your stupidity, everyone is suffering. Get it through your head.<br><br>Blah blah blah, MARY-ELLEN CATCHES THEM MAKING OUT. SCANDALOUS BECAUSE THEY'RE SUPPOSED TO BE BROTHER AND SISTER. BETHANY ERASES HER MEMORY. Done.<br><br>Blah blah blah, SEVENS ATTACK AND KILL XAVIER!<br>Wait, what?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392615ra/755826.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392615ra/755827.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THE BEST THING FROM THIS BOOK, PERIOD.<br>But it doesn't last. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/413023.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Blah blah blah, demon possession, blah blah blah, Jake is back, blah blah, Gabriel gets his wings stripped--<br><br>BLAH BLAH BLAH, I don't care.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[By the way, she meets Xavier's dead girlfriend, Emily. And Xavier is part-angel. HOLY SHIT! Way to go, Adornetto! You couldn't help but make him more special, could you? And apparently this whole mess is because he is part-angel and not because Bethany is marrying Xavier. Now that's what I call totally missing the point. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Short story short, Bethany gets back to Heaven, she finds it boring, God gets mad, she gets her wings stripped, <b>AND SHE'S FINALLY HUMAN.</b><br>Yes, you read that correctly. She gets rewarded even though she caused disaster and chaos everywhere. Such a Mary Sue.<br>Even though two years passed when she was in Heaven, Xavier and Bethany get back together and live happily ever after.<br>THE. FUCKING. END.<br><br>This was all over the place, it wasn't funny. This homophobic, sexist (There's a part where it explicitly says that women should obey their husbands), and Christianity-ruiner mess of a book is absolute trash.<br><br>And I'm glad I'm done.<br>Thanks a fucking lot for the suffering.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6295487321945903738" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_346418927" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/346418927" />
    <a title="Tarra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5160456-tarra"><img alt="Tarra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1571711185p2/5160456.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/346418927?book_show_action=true">Jun 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tarra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tarra" href="/user/show/5160456-tarra">Tarra</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=nearly-cockeyed">nearly-cockeyed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=whiney-protagonist">whiney-protagonist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=weak-protagonist">weak-protagonist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=just-shoot-me">just-shoot-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=right-under-300-pgs-within-10-pgs">right-under-300-pgs-within-10-pgs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=long-winded">long-winded</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5160456-tarra?shelf=2012">2012</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer346418927" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer845721310866753223"><i>-0 stars</i><br/><br/>Oh my. I have to say this was the worst one yet. One would believe that when someone has three tries to get something right, that person eventually would...<br/><br/>Where do I begin?<br/><br/>Let's start with the fun fact that the dense, smoky forestry in South Carolina can, in fact, hide your sinning asses from the Great Cheezus himself! Yup. Bet'cha you didn't know that. Well there you have it. So, if you sin beyond imaginable circumstances you now know where to hide your shame riddled face. And to help </span>
  <span id="freeText845721310866753223" style="display:none"><i>-0 stars</i><br /><br />Oh my. I have to say this was the worst one yet. One would believe that when someone has three tries to get something right, that person eventually would...<br /><br />Where do I begin?<br /><br />Let's start with the fun fact that the dense, smoky forestry in South Carolina can, in fact, hide your sinning asses from the Great Cheezus himself! Yup. Bet'cha you didn't know that. Well there you have it. So, if you sin beyond imaginable circumstances you now know where to hide your shame riddled face. And to help you get there: a black jeep. They can outrun angels... Oh and stay indoors. <br /><br />Also, a large college campus can hide you from angels...beings that watch you in the sky...but not at Ole Miss...<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Completely fucking stupid.</i>
</b><br /><br />It's almost as if you have to have an out of body experience as you read this or the sheer stupidity of it would do you in. Locked up, key tossed.<br /><br />This is what left me mind-bottled:<br /><br />Why did the priest that married these two assholes get killed? Beth lied to him to sway his decision to marry them saying that it was God's plan. That doesn't seem fair that he believed <i>an angel</i> and was killed. <br /><br />How was he dealt with so efficiently but Bonnie and Clyde get to resume FUBARing everyone's life they come in contact with and have been doing such FUBARing for a little over a year now?<br /><br />Why did I have to sit through 296 pages of mind numbing shenanigans from the bobsy twins?<i> why? why?</i><br /><br />Why was the Archangel Gabriel going to give up his wings for the selfish needs of an adolescent angel and her husband? and don't feed me that bullshit about "angels are supposed to protect man and that's what he was doing" because that seems pretty convenient... There is a whole wide world out there that needs a Arch not just some sniveling teenagers with bad case of the sassy-times.<br /><br />Is Heaven good or bad? I couldn't figure thay shit out.<br /><br />Does God actually know what's going on? Ever? Cuz I couldn't figure that shit out either. It was made to seem like maybe God got in a bit over his head creating the whole world...<br /><br />And for all the donuts in Springfield, Why wouldn't Beth, who said repeatedly that she'd give herself up because she wanted to take responsibility for her actions just give herself up??? Take what was coming to her like an adult and then find her way back? Boom. Story over and Adornetto doesn't have a hit out on her. <br /><br />The rascals:<br /><br />Beth. Wow, Beth. She was absurdly self centered. I felt it was more so in this book than with any other. She thought only of herself and how she would get Xavier. She didn't care about Gabriel, Ivy, Molly, anyone! Just herself. How was Beth feeling after she lied the Father Mel and got him killed? bad but she still had Xavier. How did Beth feel when Xavier had to leave his family with no explanation to follow her around? bad but she still had Xavier. How did Beth feel when the trail of bodies just kept piling up around her just because they said "Hi" to her once in passing? bad, but she still had Xavier. How about when Gabriel was getting his wings CHOPPED the fuck off and Xavier was battling Lucifer? Bad. But. She. Still. Had. Xavier. It was sickening.<br /><br />She would say she felt some emotion close to gratitude and then do something that completely contradicted it. She would flip-flop back and forth about being tired of fighting and wanting a fight. She even took on an Avatar State at one point but never once channeled it again.... fucking weird and stupid. <br /><br />Now, I have to say that I don't do the whole God thing. Personal choice. Yeah, I know, I'm going to Hell. Thank you.<br /><br /> The amount of hypocrisy in this book was difficult to swallow. Beth found some way to twist every God thing to fit her needs. She would go on and on about His will and Her Creator just so that she can explain away the unhealthy relationship she had. It was as if Adornetto didn't want to stick to her guns about what it was she exactly believed happened with religion or God. She would write one thing but turn around a chapter later and refute it... What? stay on one side. <br /><br />Xavier is part angel....humph. Seriously? Whatevs. I can't take it anymore. <br /><br />Molly was in an unhealthy relationship...per Beth. Ha. She was also shit on routinely in this book. Poor Molls.<br /><br />Gabriel and Ivy: Humph. That is all.<br /><br />Jake Thorn: Welcome back. (That whole scene was so utterly fucking unnecessary.)<br /><br />All in all: I'm so fucking happy to be done with this series that I cried. I cried on the last page. I also cried during the book at varying parts because my psyche couldn't handle the dribble anymore. <br /><br />Alexandra Adornetto,<br /><br />My disdain for you has only grown since Halo. I would ride this wave for all it's worth Honey, because your success was a fluke. I am almost afraid to think about how any of this mirrors your real life... Or worse yet, how you would want it to. Molly wasn't the only one in an unhealthy relationship. I really hope you understand that.<br /><br />One day, America will have a chance to be top billing in the world-wide race for the title of "Country with the Best Education System" and these "books" will be nothing but cinders. I hope that I am around to witness that day. Until then, I will have my own bonfire.<br /><br />Nearly Cockeyed in California.</span>
  <a data-text-id="845721310866753223" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
